# math.RT [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Simple gradable $\mathbb{C}\lbrack\mathtt{h}\rbrack$-torsion free $\mathfrak{sl}_2$-modules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19028)
*Volodymyr Mazorchuk,Shuoyang Xu*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文对一类特定的$\mathfrak{sl}_2$-模进行了显式分类和构造：这些模是有限秩的扭自由模（关于Cartan子代数的作用），并且允许一个与模秩对应的有限循环群分次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对$\mathfrak{sl}_2$-模进行分类是李代数表示论的核心问题之一。已有许多关于权模、单模的分类结果，但对于扭自由模（即作为Cartan子代数作用下的自由模）的有限秩情形，分类尚未完备。本文旨在填补这一空白，给出这类模的显式分类与构造。

Method: 作者利用有限循环群分次结构，结合$\mathfrak{sl}_2$的生成元关系，分析了模在Cartan子代数作用下的扭自由性质。通过研究分次分量上的作用关系，推导出模的结构参数，进而给出分类和显式构造。

Result: 得到了所有满足条件的$\mathfrak{sl}_2$-模的完整分类，并给出了具体的构造方法。这些模由有限秩的自由$\mathbb{C}[h]$-模（其中$h$为Cartan子代数）赋予特定的$\mathfrak{sl}_2$作用构成。

Conclusion: 完成了对一类重要的$\mathfrak{sl}_2$-模的分类和构造工作，深化了对李代数表示理论中扭自由模的理解。

Abstract: We give an explicit classification as well as an explicit construction of simple $\mathfrak{sl}_2$-modules that are torsion-free of finite rank with respect to the action of the Cartan subalgebra and which admit a grading by a finite cyclic group corresponding to the rank of the module.

</details>


<div id='math.SG'></div>

# math.SG [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Persistent Entropy of Floer Persistence Barcodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19071)
*Wenmin Gong*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文提出了Floer同调理论中的持久熵（persistent entropy），这是一种基于持久条码Shannon熵的渐近线性增长率不变量，并证明了其与条码熵在哈密顿微分同胚下的等价性，以及在不同几何背景下的计算与稳定性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受拓扑数据分析中持久条码的Shannon熵启发，作者希望在Floer同调理论中引入一个新的熵不变量，以定量方式编码动作过滤后的Floer同调信息，并补充Çineli–Ginzburg–Gürel提出的条码熵。该工作旨在建立持久熵与已有不变量之间的等价关系，并探索其在Liouville域、余切圆盘束及Reeb流等场景下的性质。

Method: 定义持久熵为迭代下有限条长度分布Shannon熵的渐近线性增长率；通过比较持久熵与条码熵，证明在哈密顿微分同胚下两者一致；利用比较不等式和次指数长度增长准则处理Liouville域的情形；计算负曲率流形余切圆盘束的持久熵，并将其与测地流拓扑熵关联；推导有限层Shannon熵的Hofer稳定性估计，并探讨Reeb流下条码熵与持久熵的刚性与柔性。

Result: 对于哈密顿微分同胚，相对和绝对持久熵与相应条码熵相等；对于Liouville域，得到一般比较不等式及在次指数长度增长条件下（超越零辛同调情形）的相等性；负曲率流形余切圆盘束的持久熵等于其测地流拓扑熵；建立了有限层Shannon熵的Hofer稳定性估计。

Conclusion: 持久熵是Floer同调理论中一个自然的熵不变量，与条码熵紧密相关但在定义上不同。它在多个几何情境下具有可计算性，并揭示了与动力系统拓扑熵的深刻联系。Hofer稳定性估计为后续刚性与柔性问题的研究提供了工具。

Abstract: Floer persistence barcodes provide a quantitative way to encode action-filtered Floer homology. Inspired by the Shannon entropy of persistence barcodes in topological data analysis, we introduce a Floer-theoretic entropy invariant, called \textit{persistent entropy}, which measures the asymptotic linear growth rate, under iteration, of the Shannon entropy determined by the distribution of finite bar lengths. This is complementary to the barcode entropy of Çineli--Ginzburg--Gürel, which records the exponential growth rate of the number of not-too-short bars. We prove that, for Hamiltonian diffeomorphisms, the relative and absolute persistent entropies coincide with the corresponding barcode entropies. For Liouville domains, we prove general comparison inequalities and a subexponential length-growth criterion which gives equality beyond the case of vanishing symplectic homology. We also compute the persistent entropy of cotangent disk bundles of negatively curved manifolds and relate it to the topological entropy of the geodesic flow. In addition, we prove Hofer-stability estimates for finite-level Shannon entropy and derive flexibility and rigidity-type questions for barcode and persistent entropies of Reeb flows.

</details>


<div id='hep-th'></div>

# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Heavenly equations in de Sitter space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14572)
*Maciej Dunajski,Timothy Moy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明所有具有非零宇宙常数的反自对偶爱因斯坦度量局部上可由Lipstein-Nagy提出的单个二阶PDE的解得到，建立了该方程与Plebański超天堂形式主义的联系并给出了Lax对，同时展示了当宇宙常数趋于零时该方程退化为Plebański第二天堂方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立具有非零宇宙常数的反自对偶爱因斯坦度量与Lipstein-Nagy方程之间的完整对应关系，填补该方程在超天堂形式主义中的理论位置，并澄清其与经典Plebański第二天堂方程在宇宙常数趋于零时的极限联系。

Method: 通过理论分析证明Lipstein-Nagy方程与反自对偶爱因斯坦度量的等价性，将该方程嵌入Plebański的超天堂形式主义框架，构造其Lax对，并在宇宙常数趋于零的极限下推导出第二天堂方程。

Result: 成功证明了Lipstein-Nagy方程完整描述了具有非零Λ的反自对偶爱因斯坦度量，建立了其在超天堂形式主义中的位置，给出了Lax对，并证明了Λ→0时退化为第二天堂方程。

Conclusion: 该工作统一了具有非零宇宙常数的反自对偶引力理论与已有可积系统框架，为理解带宇宙常数的引力理论的可积性提供了新视角。

Abstract: We demonstrate that all anti-self-dual Einstein metrics with non--zero cosmological constant $Λ$ locally arise from solutions of a single second order PDE introduced by Lipstein and Nagy. We show how this equation fits into the hyper--heavenly formalism of Plebański, and establish a Lax pair. Finally we show how Plebański's second heavenly equation arises in the limit as $Λ\rightarrow 0$.

</details>


### [4] [Meromorphic amplitudes from 3-dimensional supersymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18331)
*Federico Ambrosino,Nathan Haouzi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了超对称理论与散射振幅之间的新联系，证明Coon振幅等价于XYZ模型在非平凡边界条件下的3d $\mathcal{N}=2$半指标。3d理论在UV定义，IR流形成为Veneziano振幅的sigma模型。交叉对称性由3d $\mathcal{N}=2$镜像对称性实现。通过将导致分支割的着装因子$\mathfrak{q}^{ST}$提升为椭圆完备化，构造了Coon振幅的亚纯修正，表明无需牺牲单值性即可实现物理极点处的正性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立超对称理论与散射振幅之间的新连接，并解决Coon振幅中由于着装因子$\mathfrak{q}^{ST}$导致的分支割问题，希望在不牺牲单值性的前提下实现物理极点处的正性。

Method: 通过将Coon振幅映射为XYZ模型的3d $\mathcal{N}=2$半指标，利用3d $\mathcal{N}=2$镜像对称性（XYZ与SQED之间）实现交叉对称性。将着装因子$\mathfrak{q}^{ST}$提升为椭圆完备化形式，构造Coon振幅的亚纯修正。

Result: 成功建立了Coon振幅与3d超对称XYZ模型半指标之间的等价关系，并构造了Coon振幅的亚纯修正版本，该修正消除了分支割，同时保持了物理极点处的正性。

Conclusion: 超对称理论为散射振幅提供了新的理论框架，椭圆完备化方法表明单值性和正性可以同时实现。

Abstract: We establish a new connection between supersymmetric theories and scattering amplitudes. We show that the Coon amplitude coincides with the 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ half-index of the XYZ model with nontrivial boundary conditions. Our 3d theory, intrinsically defined in the UV, flows to a sigma model in the IR whose partition function is the Veneziano amplitude. Crossing symmetry is realized as a consequence of 3d $\mathcal{N}=2$ mirror symmetry between XYZ and SQED. We use this correspondence to construct a meromorphic modification of the Coon amplitude by promoting the long-standing dressing factor $\mathfrak{q}^{ST}$ responsible for a branch cut to an elliptic completion thereof. This illustrates that one does not have to give up single-valuedness to achieve positivity at the physical poles.

</details>


### [5] [Gauging in superconductors and other electronic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.18733)
*Marcus Berg,Andrea Cappelli,Riccardo Villa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用拓扑场论和广义对称性重新描述了s波超导体的拓扑性质，指出其在低能下表现为BF理论并具有拓扑序，同时揭示了超导体固有的引力-磁反常与Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren玻色化之间的关系，该反常禁止了低能下的平庸有质量相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的s波超导体已被认识到是拓扑物相，但其动力学规范场蕴含的全局特征尚未被充分理解。作者希望利用拓扑场论和广义对称性工具对这些系统进行更新描述。

Method: 使用拓扑场论（尤其是BF理论）和广义对称性框架，分析Higgs模型的低能极限，考虑自旋c连接以描述库珀对中费米子的自旋，并通过规范费米子宇称(-1)^F实现玻色化。

Result: 超导体本质上是玻色系统，但保留了引力-磁反常作为其费米子起源的残余；该反常与Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren玻色化相关，普遍存在于3D和4D时空的规范电子物质中，禁止低能下的平庸有质量相。

Conclusion: 该反常特征不仅适用于Higgs模型，也适用于其他类型的超导体，并出现在3D电动力学的非平庸无质量相中，具有广泛的普适性。

Abstract: Ordinary, s-wave superconductors have been recognized as being topological phases of matter, in which the dynamical gauge field implies less understood global features. Using the tools of topological field theories and generalized symmetries, we provide an updated description of these systems. At very low energies, the Higgs model reduces to the BF theory, which exhibits topological order. Furthermore, the gauge field must be a spin$_c$ connection, to describe the spin of fermions forming Cooper pairs. Gauging implies that superconductors are inherently bosonic systems, yet they are endowed with a gravito-magnetic anomaly that is the remnant of their fermionic origin. We recognize that this anomaly is related to the Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren bosonization, achieved via gauging fermion parity $(-1)^F$, now included in the gauge dynamics. This anomaly characterizes gauged electronic matter in great generality in three and four spacetime dimensions, forbidding trivial massive phases at low energy. It holds beyond the validity of the Higgs model, nd in other kinds of superconductors as well. It also appears in the nontrivial massless phase of three-dimensional electrodynamics, recently understood.

</details>


### [6] [The pole truth: an analytical graviton propagator from Asymptotic Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18343)
*Benjamin Knorr*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从渐近安全框架推导了引力子传播子的解析近似，发现在自旋-2扇区既没有额外极点，也没有幺正性或因果性破坏的迹象。研究结果支持渐近安全不引入新自由度，与广义相对论传播相同的场内容。机制在于有限阶导数展开中赝极点的残差随阶数增加趋近于零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证渐近安全框架下量子引力理论的幺正性和因果性，检验其是否引入新的非物理自由度或违反物理一致性条件。

Method: 通过解析近似方法推导渐近安全框架下的引力子传播子，分析传播子的极点结构和残差行为，研究有限阶导数展开中赝极点的收敛性质。

Result: 自旋-2扇区没有出现额外极点；没有发现幺正性或因果性违反的证据；渐近安全框架传播的场内容与广义相对论相同；有限阶导数展开中出现的赝极点残差随展开阶数增加而趋于零。

Conclusion: 渐近安全框架不引入新自由度，保持了与广义相对论相同的场内容，进一步增强了渐近安全作为量子引力候选理论的可行性。

Abstract: We derive an analytical approximation for the graviton propagator from Asymptotic Safety. We find neither extra poles nor indications of unitarity or causality violations in the spin-two sector. Our results strengthen the case that Asymptotic Safety does not introduce new degrees of freedom, and thus propagates the same field content as General Relativity. We also identify the underlying mechanism: the residues of spurious poles in finite-order derivative expansions approach zero as the order is increased.

</details>


### [7] [Black p-brane Thermodynamics without Constructing Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18344)
*Bing-Yang Han,H. Lu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将前作(2512.09930)的方法推广到任意维度中的黑色p-膜热力学（包括黑洞和弦作为特例），可在不构造相应解的情况下导出热力学量，并进一步扩展到涉及一般标量陪集的体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将前作中发展的无需显式求解即可导出热力学量的方法，从已有的特殊情形推广至更一般的黑色p-膜以及含标量陪集的系统，从而简化这类系统的热力学分析。

Method: 将前作(2512.09930)中用于黑洞热力学计算的推广方法，扩展到任意维度的黑色p-膜（包括黑洞和弦作为特例），并进一步推广到包含一般标量陪集的情况。

Result: 成功证明了无需构造相应的黑p-膜解，即可直接推导出热力学量；方法对任意维度、含标量陪集的系统均有效。

Conclusion: 该推广方法为研究黑色p-膜及更一般标量陪集系统的热力学提供了一种无需显式求解的通用框架。

Abstract: This paper generalizes the method used in the previous article 2512.09930 to black $p$-brane thermodynamics in arbitrary dimensions containing black holes and strings as special cases: thermodynamic quantities can be derived without constructing the corresponding black $p$-brane solutions. We further extend the discussion to black holes or $p$-branes involving a general scalar coset.

</details>


### [8] [Exponentiation of higher-point and higher-genus Virasoro conformal blocks in the semiclassical limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18345)
*Marius Gerbershagen,Jakob Hollweck*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了在任意通道下，高点多点函数和高亏格背景的Virasoro共形块在半经典极限（c→∞，h/c有限）下指数化，并提出了用于计算一般亏格全局共形块的新构造方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期存在的猜想声称Virasoro共形块在半经典极限下会指数化，但此前仅对球面上的四点块和环面的一点块得到证明。本文旨在将这一证明扩展到更一般的情形。

Method: 基于振子方法的创新扩展，将其推广到三条内线交汇于一个顶点的情况，从而处理更高点函数和更高亏格背景下的共形块计算。

Result: 成功将指数化证明扩展到任意通道下的一般共形块（包括高点多点函数和高亏格背景），并得到了在形式幂级数层面成立的结论。

Conclusion: 证明了Virasoro共形块在半经典极限下的指数化性质对一般情况成立，同时给出了计算二维CFT中一般亏格全局共形块的新构造方法。

Abstract: A long-standing conjecture claims that Virasoro conformal blocks exponentiate in the semiclassical limit $c \to \infty$ with $h/c$ finite. However, this has been proven only for four-point blocks on the sphere and one-point blocks on the torus. Here we extend the proof to general conformal blocks for higher-point functions and higher-genus backgrounds in arbitrary channels. The statement is to be understood at the level of a formal power series. Our proof builds upon a novel extension of the oscillator method for the computation of conformal blocks to cases where three internal lines meet at a vertex. This extension also gives a new constructive method to compute global conformal blocks in 2d CFTs at general genus.

</details>


### [9] [Ghosts versus Unstable Particles in Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18349)
*Luca Buoninfante*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过对比量子场论中的不稳定粒子与鬼场（ghost）的多粒子阈上行为，揭示了鬼场的物理本质：鬼场在渐近极限下不自发衰变，但由于与多粒子成分的干涉掩盖了其负模单粒子态，因此无法获得粒子解释；两者差异源于 dressed 传播子在复平面第一或第二黎曼叶上的不同解析结构，且鬼共振在现象学上更窄、正负能量峰之间的干涉更弱；有限时间效应进一步放大了这些差异，并识别出不同时间区域的动力学行为，支持渐近极限下不存在自由传播鬼粒子的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清鬼场（负模态）在多粒子阈以上的物理本质，区分其与不稳定粒子的行为差异，尤其是解决鬼场是否能在渐近极限下作为自由粒子传播这一概念性问题。

Method: 采用两种理论框架：（1）渐近形式化分析，利用 dressed 传播子的解析结构（复共轭极点位于第一或第二黎曼叶）区分鬼场与不稳定粒子；（2）有限时间间隔内的量子场论形式化，结合 dressed 传播子的合理近似，研究有限时间效应对共振行为的放大作用及不同时间区域的动力学。

Result: 鬼场与不稳定粒子的 dressed 传播子具有不同的黎曼叶极点结构；鬼共振在现象学上更窄，正负能量峰值干涉更弱；有限时间效应放大差异，产生更高峰值等新特征；识别出三个时间区域：短时自由粒子近似、中等时相互作用与干涉主导、长时间渐近复共轭极点对涌现；支持渐近极限下无自由传播鬼粒子的结论。

Conclusion: 鬼场与不稳定粒子本质不同：鬼场在渐近极限下存活但不衰变，但无法作为自由粒子传播；有限时间效应提供了区分鬼共振与普通共振的新现象学途径；该研究深化了对量子场论中负模态物理意义的理解。

Abstract: We elucidate the physical nature of ghosts above the multi-particle threshold by contrasting them with unstable particles in quantum field theory. We first consider the asymptotic formulation, where ordinary positive-norm one-particle states can be unstable and decay, whereas ghosts survive asymptotically without decaying, yet admit no particle interpretation due to interference with the multi-particle component which masks the negative-norm one-particle state. This distinction originates from two different analytic structures of the dressed propagator, whose complex conjugate poles lie in the first or second Riemann sheet in the ghost or ordinary case, respectively. Ghost resonances are, in principle, phenomenologically distinguishable from ordinary ones, being narrower and exhibiting weaker interference between positive- and negative-energy peaks. We then formulate the quantum field theory in a finite interval of time and, working within a suitable approximation for the dressed propagator, find that finite-time effects amplify differences in the resonant behavior and give rise to new features, such as higher peaks in ghost resonances. Distinct temporal regimes are also identified: for times shorter than the inverse width, an approximate free-particle description is valid, whereas at later times interactions and interference effects dominate, leading to decay or multi-particle masking. Complex poles in the dressed propagator emerge only at late times and become complex-conjugate pairs asymptotically, determining the asymptotic dynamics. This study supports the absence of freely propagating ghost particles in the asymptotic limit.

</details>


### [10] [Probing weak chaos in $\mathcal N=4$ super Yang-Mills and long-range spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18351)
*Pawel Caputa,Brian Creed,Rathindra Nath Das,Saskia Demulder,Tristan McLoughlin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了$\mathcal N=4$超杨-米尔斯理论及其$\beta$-形变中$\mathfrak{su}(2)$扇区平面膨胀算子的有限圈截断的量子混沌特征。在单圈级模型可积，而全圈平面理论预期也可积。通过谱统计、本征矢量诊断和展演复杂性分析，发现两圈和四圈截断在足够大耦合下呈现GOE能级统计但具有弱可积破缺特征，三圈截断未表现出混沌；本征态随机性低于GOE向量，表明弱遍历性和多重分形；Krylov空间数据与能谱统计存在关联，结果提示有限圈膨胀算子并非普通长程自旋链哈密顿量，其行为与全圈平面理论中可积性的恢复一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在可积的单圈极限和预期可积的全圈平面理论之间，研究有限圈截断中混沌行为如何涌现，探究量子混沌在可积性恢复过程中的特征。

Method: 采用谱统计（能级间距分布）、本征矢量诊断（本征态随机性分析）和展演复杂性（Krylov空间复杂度）三种方法，分析$\mathfrak{su}(2)$扇区平面膨胀算子的有限圈截断模型在耦合常数变化下的行为。

Result: 两圈和四圈截断在足够大耦合下呈现GOE能级统计但具有弱可积破缺特征，且四圈临界耦合更大；三圈截断未表现出混沌；本征态随机性低于GOE向量；Krylov空间数据与能谱统计存在关联。

Conclusion: 有限圈膨胀算子并非普通长程自旋链哈密顿量，其混沌行为特征与全圈平面理论中可积性恢复的预期一致。

Abstract: We study signatures of quantum chaos in finite-loop truncations of the planar dilatation operator in the $\mathfrak{su}(2)$ sector of $\mathcal N=4$ super Yang-Mills and its $β$-deformation. These truncations define holographically motivated long-range deformations of the nearest-neighbour XXX spin chain. At one-loop the model is integrable, while the all-loop planar theory is expected to again be integrable. Finite-loop truncations therefore provide a natural setting for investigating how chaotic behaviour emerges between these two integrable limits. We analyse this question using spectral statistics, eigenvector diagnostics and spread complexity. We find that the two- and four-loop truncations develop GOE-like level statistics at sufficiently large coupling but with features characteristic of weak integrability breaking. The integrability breaking at four-loops is weaker than at two-loops and the critical coupling at which chaos occurs is larger, at least for long spin chains. The three-loop truncation does not show the same onset of chaos in the range studied. Eigenvector diagnostics show that the corresponding eigenstates remain less random than GOE vectors, indicating weak ergodicity and multifractality. Finally, we can identify signatures of the eigenvalue and eigenvector chaos in the Krylov-space data. Namely, we demonstrate a correlation of the level spacing statistics with the peak of spread complexity and disorder on the Krylov chain. The delocalisation of the initial state in the Hamiltonian eigenbasis is shown to strongly affect the saturation of complexity. Our results suggest that finite-loop dilatation operators are not generic long-range spin chain Hamiltonians, but already display patterns consistent with the restoration of integrability in the all-loop planar theory.

</details>


### [11] [Tracing Transcendentality in Protected Correlators of N=4 SYM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18362)
*Marco S. Bianchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了N=4 SYM中受保护标量算符的两点函数，重点分析了其在维数约化下的超越性特性。通过双圈和最高经典维度10的算符显式计算，发现单圈修正具有普适性，而双圈时高维算符的均匀超越性出现可控的部分破缺，可通过算符组合完全抵消。主要结果是得到了双圈关联子在任意维度和迹结构下的完整平面外推，其依赖关系完全由算符中应力张量多重态因子的数量控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解N=4 SYM中受保护算符两点函数的超越性特性，特别是在维数约化框架下量子修正的行为，以及探索超越性破缺的可控性和可预测性。

Method: 采用维数约化方法，通过双圈微扰计算，系统分析最高经典维度10、多种迹结构的受保护标量算符的两点函数，并与局域化预言进行对比验证。

Result: 单圈修正具有普适性；双圈时高维算符出现均匀超越性的可控部分破缺，但可通过算符组合完全抵消；得到了完整的平面外推公式，其依赖关系仅由应力张量多重态因子数量决定；所有可比较的情形均与局域化预言一致。

Conclusion: 受保护算符两点函数的双圈超越性破缺是可控且可预测的，平面外推公式具有简洁的普适结构，且微扰结果与局域化预言高度吻合。

Abstract: We study two-point functions of protected scalar operators in N=4 SYM, focusing on their transcendentality properties in dimensional reduction, where quantum corrections are subleading in the regulator. We compute the correlators explicitly through two loops and operators up to classical dimension 10, for all trace structures. The one-loop correction is universal. At two loops, we find a controlled partial breaking of uniform transcendentality for higher-dimensional operators, which can be cancelled by suitable combinations of correlators in a fully predictable way. A main result is a complete planar extrapolation for two-loop correlators at arbitrary dimension and trace structure, whose dependence is entirely controlled by the number of stress-tensor multiplet factors in the operator. The perturbative results agree with localization predictions in all cases where comparisons are possible.

</details>


### [12] [What makes spacetime spin in string theory?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18380)
*Matilda Delgado,Lorenz Eberhardt,Marija Tomašević*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了II型弦论中目标时空需具备自旋结构的要求源自世界 sheet GSO投影的一致性，该一致性受混合全局反常（由自旋配边群Ω₃^spin(Bℤ₂×X)检测）约束。对于光滑目标空间，反常消失等价于X为自旋流形；对于一般轨道形[ˆX/G]，ˆX需携带G-等变自旋结构。同时分类了世界 sheet理论中所有可能的θ角，对应弦论微扰论中可见的目标空间理论的所有连续和离散背景场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清II型弦论中目标空间自旋结构要求的起源，证明该要求直接来自世界 sheet GSO投影的一致性，而非仅仅源于超对称或旋量存在的考虑。

Method: 利用自旋配边群Ω₃^spin(Bℤ₂×X)检测混合全局反常，通过计算相关混合配边群并识别GSO投影世界 sheet理论的配边类来分析反常消失条件。

Result: 光滑目标空间中反常消失条件等价于X为自旋流形；一般轨道形中ˆX需携带G-等变自旋结构。同时分类了世界 sheet理论中所有可能的θ角，对应所有连续和离散背景场。

Conclusion: II型弦论的目标空间自旋结构要求源自世界 sheet GSO投影的量子一致性，该结果统一了光滑流形和轨道形的情况，并为目标空间背景场的分类提供了世界 sheet视角。

Abstract: Type II string theory in the absence of orientifolds requires the target spacetime $X$ to admit a spin structure. We show that this familiar requirement arises directly from the consistency of the worldsheet GSO projection. The obstruction is a mixed global anomaly between $(-1)^{\text{F}_L}$ and the target space background data, detected by the spin bordism group $Ω_3^{\mathrm{spin}}(B\mathbb{Z}_2\times X)$. We compute the relevant mixed bordism group and identify the bordism class of the GSO-projected worldsheet theory. For smooth target spaces, vanishing of the anomaly reduces to the condition that $X$ is spin, while for general orbifolds $[\hat{X}/G]$, $\hat{X}$ has to carry a $G$-equivariant spin structure. We also classify all possible theta angles in the worldsheet theory and show that they correspond to all possible continuous and discrete background fields of the target space theory visible in string perturbation theory.

### [13] [An effective field theory approach to the sign problem in BFSS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18396)
*Gauri Batra,Henry W. Lin,Haifeng Tang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种有效场论方法来分析量子费米子理论中的符号问题。应用于D0-膜/BFSS矩阵量子力学时，发现连续理论在大N't Hooft regime中确实存在符号问题，但该问题在高阶高温展开（10圈阶）才显现且数值前因子很小，因此在中等耦合下对热力学量的影响较小。论文还初步将该框架推广到高维最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 费米子量子理论的经典模拟面临符号问题的严重阻碍，需要发展新的分析方法来理解和量化该问题。

Method: 提出有效场论方法：在高温下，d+1维场论约化为d维玻色理论，高维理论中Pfaffian的相位编码为低维理论中的一个算符。将该框架应用于D0-膜/BFSS矩阵量子力学，相位成为玻色多矩阵积分中的算符。

Result: 连续理论在大N't Hooft regime中确实存在符号问题；但需要在高温展开至10圈阶才显现，且相关图贡献的数值前因子很小。对于温度T≳λ^{1/3}，忽略符号问题在热力学量中仅引入较小分数误差；在更强耦合下符号问题可能变得更严重。

Conclusion: 该有效场论方法有效揭示了符号问题的结构，Pfaffian相位作为O(9)赝标量导致其延迟出现。初步推广到高维最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论，为理解更广泛理论中的符号问题提供了新途径。

Abstract: The sign problem is a notorious obstacle for classically simulating quantum theories with fermions. We propose an effective field theory method for analyzing the sign problem. At high temperatures, a $d$+1 dimensional field theory reduces to a bosonic $d$-dimensional theory; the phase of the Pfaffian in the higher dimensional theory is encoded in an operator in the lower dimensional theory. We apply this framework to the D0-brane/BFSS matrix quantum mechanics, where the phase becomes an operator in a bosonic multi-matrix integral. Our results show that the continuum theory has a sign problem that persists in the large-$N$ 't Hooft regime. However, detecting the sign problem involves going to 10-loop order in the high-temperature expansion. This delayed onset follows from the fact that the Pfaffian phase transforms as an $O(9)$ pseudoscalar. Furthermore, the relevant diagrams give a numerically small prefactor. Consequently, ignoring the sign problem leads to a relatively small fractional error in thermodynamic quantities for temperatures $T \gtrsim λ^{1/3}$. However, at stronger coupling in the 't Hooft regime, the sign problem may become more severe. Finally, we initiate the application of this framework to higher-dimensional maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theories.

### [14] [Tropical WKB asymptotics of NRS coordinates for opers in $SU(2)$, $N_f=4$ theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18452)
*Vasilii Iugov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立SL₂-opers半经典极限与Seiberg-Witten理论之间的联系，在NRS坐标框架下通过精确WKB方法严格推导渐近对应关系。

Method: 使用精确WKB连接公式、NRS Darboux坐标、热带化技术、分段整数仿射线性系统分析，以及弱耦合退化下的plumbing极限构造。

Result: 在单模且循环构成原始辛对的室中，NRS坐标的领先对数渐近与Seiberg-Witten周期（经味周期平移）一致；非单模或退化室则视为NRS图的局限。

Conclusion: 建立了特定室中NRS坐标热带极限与Seiberg-Witten周期的对应关系，但未声称全局坐标无关的恢复定理；弱耦合退化下可构造兼容的NRS图。

Abstract: We study the semiclassical limit of SL_2-opers on the four-punctured sphere in Nekrasov-Rosly-Shatashvili Darboux coordinates. Using exact Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin (WKB) connection formulae, we express the trace coordinates of the corresponding SL_2(C) character variety as finite Laurent sums of Voros exponentials. Tropicalizing these formulae and the NRS relations gives a chamberwise integer affine linear system for the leading logarithms of the NRS coordinates. In chambers where this system is unimodular and the selected cycles form a primitive symplectic pair, the leading asymptotics agree, up to flavor-period shifts, with Seiberg-Witten periods of the N=2 SU(2) theory with N_f=4 fundamental hypermultiplets. We verify this mechanism in a sample chamber and in the weak-coupling degeneration. No global coordinate-independent recovery theorem is claimed; non-unimodular or degenerate chambers are treated as limitations of the chosen NRS chart. In the weak-coupling degeneration, we show that the NRS chart can be chosen compatibly with the plumbing limit so that the resulting chamber is unimodular and non-degenerate away from tropical walls.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究广义大质量引力中翘曲黑洞的热力学稳定性，并超越经典稳定性分析，研究其热涨落行为及非平衡热力学过程。

Method: 经典稳定性分析（热容量、Davies相变曲线）+ 修正的有限时间非平衡Ruppeiner涨落理论（Hessian方法），推导等熵和等能过程中的热力学测地线方程与热力学长度。

Result: (1) 黑洞热力学不稳定，存在非平凡的Davies相变曲线；(2) 得到精确的on-shell角动量轨迹及热力学长度，可用于估计弛豫时间；(3) 热力学测地线方程不允许恒定角动量解，表明角动量连续变化；(4) 结果与拓扑大质量引力中的翘曲AdS₃黑洞极限一致。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了广义大质量引力中翘曲黑洞在经典和非平衡涨落层面上的热力学性质，为非平衡黑洞热力学提供了定量分析框架。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic stability and the stochastic thermal fluctuations of the warped black hole solution in three-dimensional General Massive Gravity. We demonstrate that the black hole is thermodynamically unstable and identify the nontrivial Davies phase-transition curves from the behavior of its admissible heat capacities. Going beyond the classical stability analysis, we study thermal fluctuations within a modified finite-time nonequilibrium extension of Ruppeiner's Hessian-based fluctuation theory. For a class of isentropic and isoenergetic processes, we derive exact on-shell angular momentum trajectories in the thermodynamic state space and compute the corresponding thermodynamic lengths. These quantities characterize relaxation processes between macrostates and provide an estimate of the associated relaxation times. Furthermore, we show that the thermodynamic geodesic equations do not admit constant-angular-momentum solutions, suggesting a continuous change of the black hole's angular momentum. Our results consistently reproduce the warped AdS$_3$ black hole limit of Topological Massive Gravity.

Method: 利用$S^d$上的超对称局域化导出微扰矩阵模型表达式，结合$\varepsilon$展开和平面对偶极限分析，并与平空间直接微扰计算进行对比验证。

Abstract: We study two-point functions of half-BPS operators in maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory continued to $d=4-2\,\varepsilon$ dimensions. Using supersymmetric localization on $S^d$, we derive perturbative matrix-model expressions for the $\varepsilon$-expansion of these correlators and obtain all-loop results at leading order in $\varepsilon$ in the planar limit, with extensions to finite-$N$ corrections and higher-charge operators. We compare the localization results with direct perturbative computations in flat space. At order $\varepsilon$ the two descriptions agree perfectly, while at higher orders our construction fails to reproduce the perturbative data due to the breaking of conformal symmetry away from four dimensions. Nevertheless, in the case of the dimension-two operator we conjecture an all-loop formula at order $\varepsilon^2$ by exploiting the precise form of the mismatch.

In addition, we implement procedures for decomposing the generated simplicial-complex matrices into simplex matrices, reconstructing the simplicial complexes of the associated pseudomanifolds from this information, and computing geometric quantities such as the volume, circumcenter, and dual-simplex volume of each simplex.

Result: 随着非厄米PT对称相互作用强度的增加，系统经历自发PT对称性破缺；其Wick旋转对应的量子淬火态展现出比标准Cardy态更大的纠缠熵增长。

Conclusion: 非厄米PT对称边界条件在全息框架下可以自然地实现，并导致超越传统结果的量子纠缠动力学行为，为理解非厄米系统中的全息和量子信息提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We present a holographic dual of a two dimensional conformal field theory with non-hermitian but Parity-Time (PT) symmetric boundary conditions, by applying the AdS/BCFT duality and by introducing an imaginary valued scalar field localized on an end-of-the-world brane. We find that as we increase the strength of the non-hermitian PT symmetric interactions, the system experiences a spontaneous PT symmetry breaking. We also consider its Wick rotated setup as a new quantum quenched state and show that its growth of entanglement entropy can be larger than the standard results obtained from standard Cardy states.

Abstract: By incorporating leading $c\,$-dependent corrections to the Carroll transformations, we introduce the ``post-Carroll transformations''. We show that, unlike the Carroll algebra, this new structure allows for a central charge in higher dimensions; we refer to it as the ``Carroll-Bargmann algebra''. To construct conformal extensions, we first build the conformal extension of the post-Carroll algebra and study field theories invariant under this symmetry. We then construct the conformal extension of the Carroll-Bargmann algebra, referred to as the ``Carroll-Schrödinger algebra'', and demonstrate that it precisely matches the symmetry algebra of the higher-dimensional Carroll-Schrödinger theory \cite{Najafizadeh:2024imn}. Finally, we derive the general form of two-point functions in a post-Carrollian CFT, which in $1+1$ dimensions exhibits both electric and magnetic sectors, while in higher dimensions only the magnetic sector survives.

### [20] [Hydrodynamics of perfect fluids with anomalies from the fermionic path integral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18779)
*Alexander G. Abanov,Andrea Cappelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文分析了带有矢量和轴矢量背景场的狄拉克费米子在红外极限附近的路径积分，在存在残余非相关流-流相互作用的情况下。积分掉费米子后，得到了一个用流表示的半经典低能有效作用量，该作用量对应于先前提出的零温度下带有反常的完美正压流体的流体动力学作用量。该方法还导出了另外两个流体动力学作用量，分别与Weyl费米子以及具有独立矢量和轴矢流的狄拉克费米子相关。这些作用量包含四维和五维的体-边界项（由于反常流入），被识别为所谓的"transgression形式"——涉及两个规范场（动力学场和背景场）的Chern-Simons形式的推广。路径积分论证为将反常纳入流体动力学所需的作用量公式化提供了"微观"解释，并阐明了从有效场论到局域流体动力学描述所需的红外约化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从微观路径积分出发，为包含反常的流体动力学有效作用量提供第一性原理推导，并阐明从有效场论到流体动力学描述的约化机制。

Method: 分析具有矢量和轴矢量背景场的狄拉克费米子路径积分，在红外极限下保留残余流-流相互作用，积分掉费米子获得半经典低能有效作用量，识别其中的transgression形式（Chern-Simons形式的推广）与反常流入的关系。

Result: 1) 获得与完美正压流体动力学作用量对应的半经典有效作用量；2) 得到Weyl费米子和独立流狄拉克费米子的两个额外流体动力学作用量；3) 识别出四维和五维体-边界项为transgression形式；4) 阐明了从有效场论到局域流体动力学描述的约化过程。

Abstract: The path integral of the Dirac fermion with vector and axial gauge backgrounds is analyzed near the infrared limit in the presence of residual irrelevant current-current interaction. After integrating out fermions, a semiclassical low-energy effective action is obtained, written in terms of currents. Its expression is found to correspond to the hydrodynamic action previously proposed for perfect barotropic fluids with anomalies at zero temperature. This approach also leads to two further hydrodynamic actions to be associated, respectively, with the Weyl fermion, and the Dirac fermion having independent vector and axial currents. These actions feature four- and five-dimensional bulk-boundary terms, owing to anomaly inflow, which are identified as being the so-called transgression forms. These are generalizations of Chern--Simons forms that involve two gauge fields: the dynamical field and the background field. The path-integral argument provides a ``microscopic'' explanation for several ingredients of the action formulation of hydrodynamics that are necessary to incorporate anomalies. It also clarifies the infrared reduction required to pass from the effective field theory to a local hydrodynamic description. This reduction is implemented by considering restricted variations of the action, familiar from hydrodynamics, which at the same time lead to four-dimensional equations of motion from the five-dimensional transgression terms.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: If entanglement wedge reconstruction is exact, then (under certain assumptions) the area term in the RT formula is a c-number, indicating that the choice of a bulk quantum state does not influence the geometry. Recently Cao, Cheng, Karthikeyan, Li, and Preskill considered a generic perturbation away from exact entanglement wedge reconstruction. The optimal reconstruction was defined; based on this, an effective area function that depends nontrivially on the quantum state was defined and its properties were analyzed. Here we make one aspect of this picture more quantitative, by showing that if as expected the area term in the RT formula is of order 1/G while the bulk entropy is of order 1, then the corrections to entanglement wedge reconstruction are exponentially small (in G) relative to corrections to the area function. Abstract: We prove a `nonlinear graviton theorem' for higher-spin self-dual gravity. Solutions of higher-spin self-dual gravity are then obtained by choosing an embedding of spacetime $\mathcal{M}$ into higher-spin space $M_{HS}$, with higher-spin symmetries arising from the different choices of embedding. Integrability of the theory is manifested in the form of a Lax pair for the system that we present. ### [23] [Universal Closed Form for Dynamical Love Numbers of Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19281)
*Mikhail P. Solon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文以封闭形式给出了Schwarzschild黑洞在任意自旋s和多极子ℓ下的动力学响应函数$\bar{F}_{\ell,s}$，该表达式通过对数重整化群方程的解并累积所有阶的Riemann zeta值实现全阶重求和，且与壳层有效场论独立验证至$\mathcal O(G^{15})$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态黑洞的Love数为零，但动力学Love数非零，此前缺乏对任意自旋和多极子下Schwarzschild黑洞动力学响应的完整封闭形式描述。

Method: 通过重整化群方程得到主导对数解$\Phi_{\ell,s}$，将运行对数提升至$\tau=\log(R_S/R)-2\sum_{k\ge2}\zeta_k\,\eta^{k-1}$实现全阶重求和；该Riemann zeta级数源于远区散射的$\Gamma(1-\eta)$因子，具有跨多极子/自旋的普适性。结果分解为视界硬匹配系数、近区反常维度和远区修饰对数三部分。使用壳层有效场论独立验证标量、电磁和引力扰动至$\mathcal O(G^{15})$。

Result: 给出$\bar{F}_{\ell,s}/4\pi R_S^{2\ell+1}=\Phi_{\ell,s}(\bar{y})-\tfrac12\eta\,\Phi_{\ell,s}'(\bar{y})$，其中$\bar{y}=-\tfrac12\eta^2\tau$，$\eta=i\omega R_S$。该结果对所有自旋$s$和多极子$\ell$均成立，且Riemann zeta值级数具有普适性。

Conclusion: 动力学响应存在因子化结构（硬匹配系数×反常维度×修饰对数），且Riemann zeta值级数本质上是Newton相位的体现，来源于远区散射的普适行为。

Abstract: Black hole static Love numbers vanish, but their dynamical counterparts do not. We present the scheme-independent dynamical response $\bar{F}_{\ell,s}$ of a Schwarzschild black hole in closed form, to all orders, and for every spin $s$ and multipole $\ell$. The result is $\bar{F}_{\ell,s}/4πR_S^{2\ell+1}=Φ_{\ell,s}(\bar{y})-\tfrac12η\,Φ_{\ell,s}'(\bar{y})$ with $\bar{y}=-\tfrac12η^2τ$ and $η=iωR_S$. Here $Φ_{\ell,s}$ is simply the leading-log solution to the renormalization group equation, but lifting the running logarithm to $τ=\log(R_S/R)-2\sum_{k\ge2}ζ_k\,η^{k-1}$ resums it to all orders. This tower of Riemann zeta values is the Newtonian phase in disguise: it originates from the same far-zone $Γ(1-η)$ that governs long-range scattering, and is universal across multipole and spin. Our result exhibits a factorization pinned to three ingredients: the hard matching coefficient at the horizon, the anomalous dimension in the near zone, and the dressed log in the far zone. Using shell effective field theory, we independently verify our formula for scalar, electromagnetic, and gravitational perturbations, reaching $\mathcal O(G^{15})$.

</details>

Abstract: In this work, we construct the simplest pseudo-Hermitian quantum field theory that is supersymmetric. This is the pseudo-Hermitian Wess-Zumino model in the sense that it contains a pair of symplectic fermions (anti-commuting scalar fields) that satisfy the Klein-Gordon equation and a spin-half boson that satisfies the Dirac equation. The conventional spin-statistics theorem is circumvented through the use of pseudo-Hermitian conjugation to define field adjoints. To make the supersymmetry manifest, we formulate the pseudo-Hermitian Wess-Zumino model using the superfield formalism. These superfields are Grassmann-odd so it is not possible to construct non-vanishing cubic interactions using only these superfields. Method: 通过图解框架（diagrammatic framework）组织大N展开中共形块展开的不同项，将交叉对称性应用于单个图解拓扑而非整个关联函数，并利用切割图（cut diagrams）分离不同的OPE数据贡献。

Result: 计算了与高迹算子相关的部分OPE数据，建立了高迹算子与低迹OPE数据之间更显式的联系，并展示了图解框架如何使这些关系更加清晰。

Conclusion: 引入的图解框架细化了大N展开中交叉对称性的应用方式，为研究体φ³和φ⁴相互作用理论中高迹算子的出现提供了系统的方法，使OPE数据的结构更加透明。

Abstract: We study four-point functions of identical scalar operators in conformal field theories with AdS duals in large-$N$ expansion. We analyze the appearance of higher-trace operators in theories dual to bulk $φ^3$ and $φ^4$ interactions, focusing on how these operators are required by crossing symmetry. We compute part of the OPE data associated with these operators. We also introduce a diagrammatic framework for organizing the different terms in the conformal block expansion within the large-$N$ expansion. This framework refines the use of crossing symmetry by allowing it to be applied to individual diagrammatic topologies, rather than only to the full correlator. It further separates different contributions to the OPE data by associating them with different cut diagrams. In this language, the emergence of higher-trace operators and their relation to lower-trace OPE data become more manifest.

</details>


### [28] [Bubble wall velocity and nucleation rates in inverse holographic phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19166)
*Francesco Bigazzi,Aldo L. Cotrone,Natalia Pinzani-Fokeeva,Tommaso Trabocchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用顶下Witten-Sakai-Sugimoto全息QCD模型，研究了强耦合下由过热驱动的一级逆相变动力学，包括未调味版本中的退禁闭相变和完整理论中禁闭相内的手征对称性恢复相变。通过计算欧几里得反弹解、泡核产生速率及过渡参数，分析了两种相变的泡壁动力学，其中退禁闭相变因自由度跃迁大导致泡壁速度参数小，而手征相变则通过稳态近似计算了泡壁速度和摩擦力。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 两种相变都找到了对应的欧几里得反弹解，并计算了泡核产生速率和过渡参数。退禁闭相变中两相自由度差异大，导致泡壁速度参数很小；手征相变中通过稳态近似得到了泡壁速度和摩擦力的具体数值。

Conclusion: 全息QCD模型可以有效描述强耦合下的一级逆相变动力学，退禁闭和手征相变在泡壁动力学上表现出不同特征，为理解相关非平衡物理提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of first-order inverse phase transitions (driven by superheating) at strong coupling, focusing on the top-down Witten-Sakai-Sugimoto model for holographic QCD. Two cases are considered: the deconfinement transition in the unflavored version of the model and a chiral symmetry-restoring transition occurring in the deconfined phase of the full theory. In both cases, we imagine driving the system into a metastable phase at high temperature, inducing the nucleation of bubbles of the stable phase. For both classes of transitions, we find the corresponding Euclidean bounce solutions and compute the bubble nucleation rates and the relevant transition parameters. For the deconfinement transition, the large jump in the number of degrees of freedom between the two phases suggests that the bubble wall velocity is parametrically small; we provide a rough estimate of it near the critical temperature. In the case of the chiral transition, instead, we compute the bubble wall velocity and the friction force exerted on the bubbles employing motivated ansatze and approximations for the steady-state configurations.

### [30] [A Dispersive Bootstrap for the Virasoro-Shapiro Amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19283)
*Yongjun Xu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用色散S矩阵自举方法研究闭弦树级Virasoro-Shapiro振幅，通过解析性、交叉对称性、分波幺正性和Regge有界性等约束，在十维最大超对称四点振幅中推导出色散关系和交叉零约束，对低能Wilson系数给出数值界限。引入Virasoro启发的非线性约束后，允许区域缩小至Virasoro-Shapiro轨迹附近；进一步在去除引力极点后的简化问题中，非线性约束将允许区域压缩至包含Virasoro-Shapiro点的小岛，并给出了解析自举解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用S矩阵自举方法，在不依赖微扰弦理论具体细节的前提下，从第一性原理（解析性、幺正性、交叉对称性和Regge行为）出发，验证和推导闭弦散射振幅（Virasoro-Shapiro振幅）的唯一性，探索弦理论在散射振幅层面是否可由基本物理原理唯一确定。

Method: 采用色散S矩阵自举框架，在十维最大超对称四点振幅中施加解析性、交叉对称性、分波幺正性和Regge有界性条件；显式保留无质量引力子极点，推导色散关系和交叉零约束，得到低能Wilson系数的数值界限；引入Virasoro启发的非线性关系进一步约束参数空间；最后在去除引力极点后的简化问题中施加非线性约束，将允许区域压缩至包含Virasoro-Shapiro点的小岛。

Result: 在完整问题中，Virasoro启发的非线性约束将允许区域缩小至Virasoro-Shapiro轨迹附近；在去除引力极点后的简化问题中，非线性约束将允许区域压缩至一个包含Virasoro-Shapiro点的小岛，且该结果可由解析自举方法解释。

Conclusion: S矩阵自举方法能够有效约束弦振幅的低能系数，结合非线性约束后可唯一确定Virasoro-Shapiro振幅，表明弦理论的散射振幅可能由基本物理原理唯一确定。

Abstract: We study the closed-string tree-level Virasoro-Shapiro amplitude using the dispersive S-matrix bootstrap. For the ten-dimensional maximally supersymmetric four-point amplitude, we impose analyticity, crossing symmetry, partial-wave unitarity, and Regge boundedness. With the massless graviton pole kept explicitly, the resulting dispersion relations and crossing null constraints give numerical bounds on the leading low-energy coefficients normalized by the gravitational coupling. We then introduce a Virasoro-inspired ansatz, which becomes a set of nonlinear relations among Wilson coefficients and shrinks the allowed region toward the Virasoro-Shapiro trajectory. Finally, we study a gravity-pole-subtracted setup, where the regular part of the amplitude has a well-defined forward limit. In this stripped problem, the nonlinear constraints reduce the allowed region to a small island containing the Virasoro-Shapiro point, for which we provide an analytic bootstrap explanation.

</details>

### [31] [Weak corrections to Minimal Dark Matter annihilations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18335)

TL;DR: 本文计算了费米子最小暗物质多重态湮灭截面的单圈弱修正，发现红外发散在热 relic丰度相关的s波组合中抵消，而速度压低的截面受到Sudakov/Sommerfeld相互作用的红外增强修正，修正幅度随多重态尺寸增大，在Higgsino-like二重态、wino-like三重态和稳定五重态等最受关注的模型中约为5%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用单圈弱修正计算，对s波（主导成分）和速度压低成分分别处理，分析了红外发散在s波中的抵消机制以及Sudakov/Sommerfeld效应对速度压低截面的增强作用。

Conclusion: 单圈弱修正对最小暗物质模型的精确重构有重要意义，特别是在Higgsino、wino和五重态等最受理论驱动的候选者中，修正量约为5%，需在理论预言中加以考虑。

Abstract: We compute the one-loop weak corrections to the annihilation cross sections of fermionic Minimal Dark Matter multiplets. Infrared divergences cancel in the dominant $s$-wave combination relevant for the thermal relic abundance. Instead, infrared-enhanced corrections affect velocity-suppressed rates, through a Sudakov/Sommerfeld interplay. The corrections grow with the multiplet size and are at the $5\%$ level in the most motivated cases: the Higgsino-like doublet, the wino-like triplet, the stable quintuplet.

### [32] [Standard Candles for Supernova Neutrino Detection at DUNE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18337)

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DUNE探测器对超新星电子中微子具有独特探测能力，但νe-Ar反应截面的不确定度严重限制了从超新星中微子通量中提取谱参数的精度，需要减少对不精确核模型的依赖。

Method: 提出数据驱动策略，利用两种标准烛光——^8B太阳中微子（约束低能部分）和停束μ子衰变中微子（约束高能部分）——来校准νe-Ar截面，从而降低核模型不确定性对超新星谱参数提取的影响。

Result: 该方法可将核模型导致的超新星谱参数提取偏差从高达300%显著降低。

Conclusion: 所提数据驱动校准策略能有效抑制核模型不确定性，提升DUNE从超新星中微子信号中提取谱参数的可靠性。

Abstract: The Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment (DUNE) far detector is sensitive to $\mathcal{O}(10)$ MeV electron neutrinos through $ν_e$ charged-current reaction with argon. This capability is a unique window into the $ν_e$ component of a Galactic core-collapse supernova flux. Extracting the properties of the supernova spectrum is, however, limited by the poorly-known $ν_e$-Ar cross section. We propose a data-driven strategy that leverages $^8$B solar neutrinos and muon-decay-at-rest neutrinos as standard candles for this process. These calibration samples constrain both the low-energy and high-energy components of the cross section relevant for supernova detection. Our method reduces the reliance on nuclear models, which can bias the extraction of the spectral parameters by as much as 300$\%$.

### [33] [Self-Calibration of the Neutrino-Argon Cross Section with Solar Neutrinos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18347)
*Rasmi Hajjar,Obada Nairat,John F. Beacom*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，利用太阳中微子数据本身，可以将DUNE实验中MeV能区$ν_e+\mathrm{^{40}Ar}$ charged-current反应截面的测量精度提升至$\lesssim$2%（9-15 MeV），远超现有直接测量~50%的不确定性。该方法依赖于独立已知的$^8$B通量与存活概率，以及Fermi和Gamow-Teller跃迁的不同角分布特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DUNE的MeV物理项目高度依赖于$ν_e+\mathrm{^{40}Ar}$ CC截面的高精度知识。现有间接约束约10%，而直接测量不确定性高达~50%，远不能满足超新星和大气中微子研究的精度需求。

Method: 利用太阳中微子数据本身进行测量，关键依赖：(1)独立已知的$^8$B中微子通量和存活概率；(2)Fermi和Gamow-Teller跃迁具有不同的角分布特征。提出两种提取跃迁强度的方法：直观分组法和主成分分析法（PCA）。

Result: 在悲观的探测假设（但探测器不确定性可控）下，9-15 MeV能区可实现$\lesssim$2%的截面测量精度。

Conclusion: 该方法为DUNE MeV物理提供了重要基础，并可推广至数十MeV能区。尽管更高能区因核碎裂通道导致复杂度显著增加，但降低不确定性对超新星和大气中微子研究至关重要。

Abstract: The success of DUNE's MeV physics program depends upon high-precision knowledge of the charged-current (CC) $ν_e+\mathrm{^{40}Ar}$ cross section. While there are indirect constraints at the 10% level for the nuclear transitions that constitute this cross section, the only direct measurement in the MeV range has an uncertainty of $\sim$50%. We show, surprisingly, that the cross section can be precisely measured using the solar-neutrino data themselves. This is possible because of independent knowledge of the $^8$B flux and survival probability, plus the distinctive angular distributions of the Fermi and Gamow-Teller transitions that comprise the cross section. We propose new methods to extract the transition strengths, considering both intuitive groupings and a Principal Component Analysis. Under pessimistic assumptions about detection, but taking detector uncertainties to be controlled, we demonstrate that a precision of $\lesssim$2% on the cross section can be achieved in the 9-15 MeV energy range. These results will be an important foundation for studying the cross section up to several tens of MeV, where the complexity increases significantly due to nuclear breakup channels but where reducing uncertainties is critical for supernova and atmospheric neutrino studies.

### [34] [The Landscape of Composite Higgs Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18364)
*Daniel Murnane*

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了复合希格斯模型中的自然性（naturalness）问题，提出了新的贝叶斯调谐度量，并对最小4D复合希格斯模型及其扩展进行了全局拟合和排除界限分析，包括轻子复合模型和暗物质候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型虽然精确，但希格斯粒子的参数需要极其精细的调谐才能解释宇宙结构的形成和生命的存在，这种"幸运巧合"令人困惑。本文旨在寻找一个更自然的解释，即不需要过度精细调谐的理论框架。

Method: 1. 提出基于贝叶斯框架的新型调谐度量（tuning measure）；2. 对最小4D复合希格斯模型（M4DCHM）进行全局拟合；3. 探索扩展模型：轻子M4DCHM（复合tau轻子嵌入不同表示）和次最小4DCHM（引入暗物质候选者）。

Result: 对M4DCHM的全局拟合给出了强排除界限；分析了不同扩展方案对自然性的改善程度；定义了这些扩展对复合希格斯扇区自然性的具体贡献。

Conclusion: 本文量化了复合希格斯模型及其扩展在改善自然性方面的实际收益，为后续探索更自然的超越标准模型物理提供了定量依据。

Abstract: While the Standard Model (SM) of particle physics contains the most precise set of predictions ever devised by humanity, that precision comes at a cost. The strange nature of the Higgs particle requires its parameters to be tuned so precisely that if the SM is indeed the true description of reality, one is forced to wonder how such a miracle as galactic structure and life could occur. Instead, we search in this work for a natural explanation. The concept of naturalness is comprehensively explored, and a new tuning measure proposed, with an aim to place it on well-defined Bayesian footing. We then turn this measure on to the analysis of a class of intriguing new physics - Composite Higgs models. These effective models are the result of a plethora of underlying theories, and they allow the production of a naturally light Higgs particle, appearing as the SM Higgs at low energy. We establish the background required to appreciate the N-site 4D Composite Higgs model, and subsequently focus on the simplest incarnations of this class. A global fit is performed on the Minimal 4D Composite Higgs model (M4DCHM), with strong exclusion bounds placed on collider search channels. We analyse any improvement in tuning that could be gained from several extensions to this model. The Leptonic M4DCHM is explored, with a composite tau lepton embedded in various representations. The possibility of a dark matter candidate existing in the Next-to-Minimal 4DCHM is considered. Ultimately, we are able to define what, if any, benefit to naturalness can come to the Composite Higgs sector by introducing these extensions.

</details>

Method: 提出领域无关的上下文感知压力测试管线，允许重建响应依赖全局参数；采用无监督区域映射框架对违反局部假设的区域进行识别和校正。

Abstract: The fast reconstruction and detector-simulation pipelines are widely used in different scientific domains, such as, in High Energy Physics (HEP) and medical imaging, where the full experimental or the device-level simulation is computationally challenging. Instead of the use of the global data context, these pipelines use simplified response models which assume reconstruction uncertainty relies on local input parameters. To probe the robustness of the local assumption, a domain-agnostic context-aware stress testing pipeline is introduced, and a reconstruction response depending on the global parameters is also allowed. For an instance in HEP at High-Luminosity LHC (HL-LHC) simulation, this work shows that the decay channel $Z \rightarrow \ell\ell$, as a benchmark, violates the local assumption resulting in a significant reconstruction bias and resolution degradation. Using the unsupervised regime-mapping framework, this work also restores this peak stability and recovers the truth-level resolution, where a robust diagnostic tool for next-generation fast simulation pipelines is accommodated.

### [36] [$π^0$-$γ$ mixing in the presence of a strong magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18507)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究强磁场下π^0介子与光子之间的混合效应，验证该效应对π^0质量及π-夸克耦合的影响程度，澄清与已有文献结果的分歧。

Method: 采用双味Nambu-Jona-Lasinio模型，在均匀外磁场背景下计算π^0与不同极化光子的混合幅，分析混合对π^0质量和π-夸克耦合常数的修正。

Result: 只有一种光子极化态能与π^0混合；在磁场强度高达1 GeV^2/e时，混合效应对π^0质量和π-夸克耦合的修正低于15%，远小于先前文献报道的结果。

Conclusion: 强磁场下π^0-光子混合效应较小，不会显著改变π^0的性质，此前文献可能高估了该效应。

Abstract: We analyze the mixing between the $π^0$ meson and the photon in the presence of a strong uniform magnetic field, in the context of a two-flavor Nambu-Jona-Lasinio model. It is shown that only one specific photon polarization state can get mixed with the $π^0$ state, a fact that can be understood on general grounds. For magnetic fields with values up to 1 GeV$^2$/e, it is found that the effect of the mixing on the pion mass and pion-quark couplings is relatively small (below a level of 15%), which is at variance with previous results reported in the literature.

### [37] [Semi-leptonic decays $B \to D^{(*)}(1S,2S)\ell ν_{\ell}$ within the covariant light-front approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18576)
*Zhi-Jie Sun,Zhi-Qing Zhang,Shi-Chen Xue,Feng-Zhou Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在协变光前夸克模型（CLFQM）框架下，系统分析了B(s)→D(s)(1S,2S)ℓν_ℓ和B(s)→D*(s)(1S,2S)ℓν_ℓ（ℓ=e,μ,τ）的半轻衰变。计算表明，轻子为e,μ时分支比与实验数据吻合良好，而τ通道的分支比系统性地小于实验测量值，解释了R(D)和R(D*)反常。预测的R(D)=0.261±0.013和R(D*)=0.228±0.026分别与HFLAV世界平均值存在3.1σ和2.1σ偏差，但与LHCb最新测量仅偏离0.16σ和1.5σ。激发态衰变分支比在10^{-4}~10^{-3}量级，与相对论夸克模型结果一致。此外还计算了前后不对称性和纵向极化分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 系统研究B(s)介子到基态和激发态D(s)与D*(s)介子的半轻衰变，解释R(D)和R(D*)实验与标准模型预测之间的反常，并在CLFQM框架下提供理论预测。

Method: 采用协变光前夸克模型（CLFQM）计算B(s)→D(s)(1S,2S)和B(s)→D*(s)(1S,2S)跃迁的形状因子，进而计算分支比、前后不对称性和纵向极化分数等物理量。

Result: 轻子为e,μ时分支比与实验数据吻合；τ通道分支比系统性偏小。R(D)和R(D*)预测值与HFLAV平均值偏差分别为3.1σ和2.1σ，与LHCb最新测量仅偏离0.16σ和1.5σ。激发态衰变分支比在10^{-4}~10^{-3}量级，与BS方程结果差异大但与RQM一致。

Conclusion: CLFQM能够较好地描述B(s)→D(s)/D*(s)半轻衰变，τ通道的系统性偏差自然解释了R(D)和R(D*)反常。激发态衰变的理论预测需要更多实验检验。

Abstract: We present a systematic analysis of the semi-leptonic decays $B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(1S,2S)\ellν_\ell$ and $B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(1S,2S)\ellν_\ell$ with $\ell=e,μ,τ$ within the covariant light-front quark model (CLFQM). Using the form factors of the transitions $B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(1S,2S)$ and $B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(1S,2S)$, we calculate the branching ratios of the relevant semi-leptonic decays and find that $Br(B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}\ell^\primeν_{\ell^\prime})$ and $Br(B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}\ell^\primeν_{\ell^\prime})$ with $\ell^\prime=e,μ$ are agree well with the data, while $Br(B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}τν_τ)$ and $Br(B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}τν_τ)$ are systematically smaller than the experimental measurements. This naturally gives rise to the so-called $\mathcal{R}(D)$ and $\mathcal{R}(D^*)$ anomalies. Our predictions $\mathcal{R}(D)=0.261\pm0.013$ and $\mathcal{R}(D^*)=0.228\pm0.026$ show $3.1σ$ and $2.1σ$ deviations from the current experimental world averages compiled by the Heavy Flavor Averaging Group (HFLAV), respectively, yet only deviate by $0.16σ$ and $1.5σ$ from the latest LHCb measurements. For the decays $B_{(s)}\to D_{(s)}(2S)\ellν_\ell$ and $B_{(s)}\to D^*_{(s)}(2S)\ellν_\ell$, their branching ratios lie in the range $10^{-4}\sim10^{-3}$, which are much larger than the results from the Bethe Salpeter (BS) equation , but agree with the relativistic quark model (RQM) calculations. Furthermore, we also calculate the forward-backward asymmetries $\mathcal{A}_{FB}$ and longitudinal polarization fractions $f_L$ for the corresponding decays. Our predictions are consistent with most other theoretical results and experimental data

### [38] [Analysis of $J/ψ$ and $ψ(2S)$ Charmonium Production in Ultraperipheral Lead-Lead and Proton-Lead Collisions at LHC Energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18595)

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于双胶子交换模型的光产生截面，利用STARlight程序系统研究了LHC能量下PbPb和pPb碰撞中的粲偶素超边缘碰撞（UPC）过程。通过引入唯象抑制因子修正理论预测，使其与PbPb碰撞的快速率和横动量分布实验数据吻合，并成功再现了快速率分布的双峰结构；而在pPb碰撞中未观察到显著抑制。研究验证了双胶子交换模型在粲偶素UPC研究中的适用性，并为未来实验设计提供了唯象指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于双胶子交换模型对J/ψ和ψ(2S)光产生截面的描述，使用STARlight程序模拟PbPb和pPb碰撞中的粲偶素UPC过程；引入唯象抑制因子修正理论结果，并与实验数据对比。

Result: 修正后的预测在TeV能级下与PbPb碰撞实验数据在不确定度内吻合，成功再现了快速率分布的双峰结构；pPb碰撞中未观测到显著抑制；横动量分布与实验的相干产生衍射图案匹配，但总产额仍略有高估。

Abstract: The two gluon exchange model serves as a key framework for describing the photoproduction of heavy vector mesons, and the photoproduction cross sections derived from it provide essential input for studies of Ultra-Peripheral Collisions (UPCs). Building on the model successful description of $J/ψ$ and $ψ(2S)$ photoproduction in previous work, we use the STARlight program to systematically investigate charmonium UPCs in PbPb and $p$Pb collisions at LHC energies. To reduce discrepancies between theoretical predictions and experimental data for rapidity and transverse momentum distributions in PbPb collisions, a phenomenological suppression factor is introduced to correct the theoretical results. We find that, in the TeV energy range, the corrected predictions agree well with experimental data within uncertainties and successfully reproduce the characteristic double-peak structure in rapidity distributions. In contrast, no significant suppression is observed in $p$Pb UPCs, which reflects the asymmetric photon fluxes and the dominant contribution from the photoproduction interaction branch. The transverse momentum distributions from STARlight simulations also match the diffractive pattern of coherent production seen experimentally, although the overall yield remains slightly overpredicted. This work further validates the applicability of photoproduction cross sections from the two gluon exchange model for charmonium UPC studies, and offers valuable phenomenological guidance for future experimental design and data analysis in UPC measurements of charmonium production.

### [39] [Semi-invisible Hyperon Decays in the Effective Lagrangian Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18652)

Method: 采用有效拉氏量方法，计算超子半不可见衰变中涉及末态相互作用的单圈三角形图的一圈强子贡献，并与树图结果进行比较。

Conclusion: 超子半不可见衰变在Mesogenesis机制下具有可观测的分支比，为实验探测提供了可能；圈图效应是精确预言的必要组成部分。

Abstract: We systematically investigate the semi-invisible decays of hyperons (hyperon $\to π(/γ)\ +$ invisible($ψ$)) in the Mesogenesis mechanism by the effective Lagrangian approach. The one-loop hadronic contribution of triangle diagrams with final-state interactions is fully examined in the present work. Our analysis indicates that the triangle diagram yield sizable corrections to the branching ratio that are as significant as those from tree diagrams. Especially for the $Σ^-\to π^-ψ$ and $Ξ^0 \to π^0 ψ$, their loop contributions cannot be ignored. Consequently, the branching ratios of hyperon hadronic semi-invisible decays are found to be of order $10^{-5}$, particularly for $Σ^+\toπ^+ψ$, $Ξ^0\toπ^0ψ$, and $Ξ^-\toπ^-ψ$, whereas those of radiative semi-invisible decays are less than $10^{-7}$.

TL;DR: 本文提出一种动力学机制，通过在早期宇宙中引入一个新标量场产生瞬时的CP破缺偏置，使CP畴壁衰变，同时保证低能CP结构完好，并将该标量场的相干振荡自然解释为暗物质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自发CP破缺（SCPV）是解决强CP问题的吸引人方案，但暴胀后形成的CP畴壁要求宇宙最高温度低于CP破缺标度，这一宇宙学约束非常严格。作者旨在消除这一约束，同时避免引入永久性的显式CP破缺。

Method: 引入一个新的标量场，该场在早期宇宙中获得具有非平凡相位的大场值，通过与CP破缺标量场的高维相互作用，在简并的CP真空间产生瞬时的偏置，从而触发CP畴壁的衰变。当新场演化至原点时偏置消失，低能CP结构保持不变。

Result: 导出了畴壁成功衰变的条件，识别了可行的参数空间，并指出新标量场的相干振荡可自然作为暗物质存在。

Conclusion: 该动力学机制有效消除了SCPV的宇宙学约束，无需永久CP破缺，同时将CP畴壁问题的解决与暗物质起源联系起来，提供了一个统一的理论框架。

Abstract: Spontaneous CP violation (SCPV) provides an attractive solution to the strong CP problem. However, SCPV after inflation suffers from the formation of CP domain walls, requiring the maximal temperature of the Universe to lie below the CP-breaking scale. In the present work, we then propose a dynamical mechanism that removes this cosmological constraint without introducing permanent explicit CPV. We consider a new scalar field that acquires a large field value with a nontrivial phase in the early Universe and induces a transient bias among degenerate CP vacua through a higher-dimensional interaction with a CP-breaking scalar field. This bias triggers the decay of CP domain walls after they form. As the new scalar field evolves toward the origin, the bias disappears, leaving the low-energy CP structure intact. We derive the conditions for successful domain wall decay and identify the viable parameter space. Furthermore, we point out that the coherent oscillation of the new scalar field naturally survives as dark matter, linking the resolution of the CP domain wall problem to the origin of dark matter.

Using the spin density matrix formalism, we trace the polarization from the initial beams through the production chain \(e^+e^- \to ψ(2S) \to γχ_{cJ}\) to the final-state baryon-antibaryon system. The helicity amplitude analysis for \(χ_{c1} \to B\bar{B}\) confirms the universal angular distribution parameter \(α= -1/3\), as dictated by the charge-conjugation helicity selection rule. For \(χ_{c2}\) decays, \(α\) and the transverse polarization depend on two independent amplitudes, and our quark-model calculations agree with existing data. Abstract: We study diffractive photo- and electroproduction of the $S$-wave heavy quarkonia $J/ψ$, $ψ(2S)$, and $Υ(nS)$ at energies relevant for the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC). The production amplitude is evaluated while retaining the full transverse-momentum ($\ell_t$) dependence of the hard two-gluon kernel, that is, without expanding the impact-parameter Bessel kernel as is done in the small-size color-dipole limit. The quarkonia light-cone wave functions are built from Cornell-potential solutions of the Schrödinger equation, normalized to the measured leptonic widths, and combined with a modern collinear gluon distribution. After benchmarking the framework against the full set of HERA charmonium cross-section ratio data, we provide a consistent set of bottomonium cross-section ratio predictions in EIC kinematics. We find that the full $\ell_t$-resolved treatment systematically improves the description of the radially excited states relative to the leading dipole limit, and we identify the kinematic windows where this difference is largest.

*Tao-Ran Hu,Hai-Long Fu,Feng-Kun Guo,Ulf-G. Meißner,Xu Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在无穷体积三体幺正框架下研究$I^G(J^{PC})=0^+(1^{++})$的$K\bar Kπ$系统，聚焦$f_1(1285)$和$f_1(1420)$共振态的极点结构。通过拟合BESIII实验数据并解析延拓到非物理黎曼面，发现$f_1(1285)$来自裸态 dressing，而$f_1(1420)$主要是动力学产生的$K\bar K^*$ S波准束缚态，支持其强子分子态解释。另发现一个由$P$波$πa_0$接触作用产生的额外极点，但对物理线形影响极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究$f_1(1285)$和$f_1(1420)$共振态的极点结构及其产生机制，澄清$f_1(1420)$是否可被解释为强子分子态，并考察三体幺正性中三角奇点机制的作用。

Method: 在无穷体积三体幺正框架下，采用旁观者-同位旋表示构建耦合的$πa_0$-$K\bar K^*$振幅，其中单粒子交换相互作用由三体幺正性自动包含三角奇点机制。短程三体相互作用通过拟合BESIII实验的$J/ψ\toγ(K^0_SK^0_Sπ^0)$衰变中$0^+(1^{++})$分量的$K^0_SK^0_Sπ^0$不变质量分布来约束。将拟合振幅解析延拓到非物理黎曼面以确定极点位置。

Result: 得到$f_1(1285)$极点为$(1277±2±1)-i(12±1±0)$ MeV，$f_1(1420)$极点为$(1435±2±7)-i(40±2±1)$ MeV。$f_1(1285)$由裸态 dressing 产生，$f_1(1420)$主要为动力学产生，可追溯到$S$波$K\bar K^*$准束缚态与附近裸态的混合。另发现一个由$P$波$πa_0$接触作用单独产生的额外极点，但对物理线形影响很小。

Conclusion: $f_1(1420)$具有强子分子态特征，主要由动力学机制产生；$f_1(1285)$则来源于裸态。三体幺正框架能有效描述这些共振结构，且三体割对积分方程解有重要影响。

Abstract: We study the $I^G(J^{PC})=0^+(1^{++})$ $K\bar Kπ$ system in an infinite-volume three-body unitary framework, focusing on the pole content of the region of the $f_1(1285)$ and $f_1(1420)$ resonances. The coupled $πa_0$-$K\bar K^*$ amplitude is constructed in the spectator-isobar representation, where the one-particle-exchange interaction required by three-body unitarity automatically incorporates the triangle-singularity mechanism. The short-range three-body interaction is constrained by fitting the $0^+(1^{++})$ component of the BESIII $K^0_SK^0_Sπ^0$ invariant-mass distribution in the $J/ψ\toγ(K^0_SK^0_Sπ^0)$ decay. Analytically continuing the fitted amplitude to the relevant unphysical Riemann sheets, we find two robust poles: \begin{align} \sqrt{s_{f_1(1285)}}&= \left(1277\pm2\pm1\right) -i\left(12\pm1\pm0\right)\text{MeV}\,,\notag\\ \sqrt{s_{f_1(1420)}}&= \left(1435\pm2\pm7\right) -i\left(40\pm2\pm1\right)\text{MeV}\,.\notag \end{align} The pole trajectories indicate that the $f_1(1285)$ originates from dressing a bare state introduced in the potential. In contrast, the $f_1(1420)$ is predominantly dynamically generated, and a single-channel analysis traces it to an $S$-wave $K\bar K^*$ quasi-bound state mixed with the nearby bare state, supporting its hadronic-molecule interpretation. We also find an additional pole deeper in the complex plane in the best-fit amplitude on the same Riemann sheet as the $f_1(1285)$. This additional pole is generated by the $P$-wave $πa_0$ contact interaction alone. It has a sizable cutoff and two-body-input dependence, and leaves little visible imprint on the physical lineshape. Finally, we provide a detailed and pedagogical appendix on how three-body cuts affect the solution of the integral equation.

</details>

Method: 计算维度八SMEFT中玻色子和双费米子算符到双费米子算符的单圈混合。

Abstract: We discuss how the $Z'$-boson of the $B-L$ Supersymmetric (SUSY) Standard Model (BLSSM) could evade the current lower bound of around 5 TeV on the mass of such a resonance (of sequential nature) from the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) by a significant margin. This happens when the experimental sensitivities are critically impaired as the $Z'$-boson becomes `fat' or develops some leptophobia or possesses an optimally large decay Branching Ratio (BR) to BLSSM-specific states (including the SUSY ones) or when some or all of these are at play simultaneously. We describe how such a $Z'$-boson could acquire there features while still respecting the non-negotiable precision constraints from the LEP and the SLC experiments running at the $Z$-pole as well as those from the multi-purpose experiments at the LHC that search for such a resonance. We explore the interplay of the aforementioned phenomena and identify the regions of the BLSSM parameter space that give rise to the described situation by carrying out a thorough scan of it. We find that $M_{Z'}$ masses as low as 2.24 TeV may still be allowed in the BLSSM under favorable circumstances.

### [47] [Tripartite Entanglement in $e^+ e^- \to t \bar{t} Z$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11296)
*Dorival Gonçalves,Alberto Navarro,Kazuki Sakurai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究未来正负电子对撞机中 $e^+e^-\to t \bar{t} Z$ 过程的 tripartite 自旋纠缠，利用完整 $12\times 12$ 自旋密度矩阵分析纠缠结构，发现集体纠缠和真正多体纠缠在集成更多运动学信息时减弱，集体纠缠在极化轻子对撞机中可观测，但真正多体纠缠的验证更具挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高能对撞中多体纠缠这一独特的量子关联现象，特别是 tripartite 自旋系统（$t,\bar{t},Z$）的纠缠结构，拓展对撞机中量子纠缠研究的维度。

Method: 基于标准模型螺旋度振幅重建完整的 $12\times 12$ 自旋密度矩阵，通过一对一 negativity、一对多 negativity 和真正多体 negativity 表征纠缠结构，在三个递进的相空间积分水平上评估，并假设在 $\sqrt{s}=1$ TeV 的全轻子衰变通道中进行量子层析。

Result: 成对纠缠通常被集体（一对多）和真正多体纠缠所抑制，所有纠缠度量在集成更多运动学信息时均下降。集体纠缠在极化高亮度轻子对撞机中可及，但真正多体纠缠仅在特定极化基准下、在 ILC 预期亮度内具有有限灵敏度。

Conclusion: $e^+e^-\to t \bar{t}Z$ 是高能碰撞中探测多体纠缠的吸引人平台，本文建立了适用于任意 tripartite 自旋系统的一般混合态框架。

Abstract: Multipartite entanglement is a uniquely quantum form of correlation that captures collective properties of a composite quantum state beyond those encoded in its bipartite subsystems. We investigate this phenomenon in the process $e^+e^-\to t\bar tZ$ at a future lepton collider, where the final state spins span the tripartite Hilbert space $\mathscr{H} = \mathbb{C}^2 \otimes \mathbb{C}^2 \otimes \mathbb{C}^3$. Starting from the Standard Model helicity amplitudes, we reconstruct the full $12\times 12$ spin density matrix and characterise its entanglement structure through one-to-one negativities, one-to-other negativities, and the genuine multipartite negativity, evaluated at three increasingly inclusive levels of phase space integration. Pairwise entanglement is generally suppressed relative to the collective (one-to-other) and the genuine multipartite entanglement, and all measures decrease as more kinematic information is integrated out. Assuming quantum tomography in the fully leptonic decay channel at $\sqrt{s}=1$ TeV, we find that collective entanglement should be accessible at a realistic high-luminosity polarised lepton collider. By contrast, certifying genuine multipartite entanglement is more challenging, with only limited sensitivity projected for a specific polarisation benchmark within the expected ILC luminosity. The study establishes $e^+e^-\to t \bar{t}Z$ as an attractive laboratory for probing multipartite entanglement in high-energy collisions and provides a general mixed state framework that applies to any tripartite spin system.

  <summary>Details</summary>

While dissipation tends to stabilize the dynamics, we question if and how environmental quantum fluctuations can generate chaos in an otherwise classically non-chaotic system. We work out a paradigmatic model of quantum optics: the dissipative Dicke model, where a large spin interacts with a dissipative harmonic mode. We dial in the classical/quantum correspondence by working in the semiclassical regime at large but finite spin. We demonstrate that, starting from a classically regular phase space in the superradiant regime, quantum noise can generate a strange attractor with fractal dimension and a positive Lyapunov exponent. We unveil the deep connection with shear-induced chaos that was recently developed in the mathematical community.

### [50] [Probing chaos and thermalization through out-of-time-ordered correlators in random field spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18982)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过数值模拟随机场海森堡自旋-1/2链中OTOC的动力学行为，分析从可积到混沌交叉的参数区域，并利用长程谱统计（如数方差）表征近饱和区的量子混沌。

Result: 可积系统OTOC饱和趋近呈1/t幂律松弛；混沌系统呈现高次幂律(1/t^α, α≥1)后接指数松弛；长程谱统计在近饱和区更有效；松弛区对随机场实现敏感而初始加扰区鲁棒；通过ETH推导了OTOC长时间饱和的精确表达式。

Conclusion: OTOC的弛豫动力学可有效区分可积与混沌体系，不同动力学区域具有普适特征，ETH可准确描述OTOC的长时间饱和行为。

Abstract: Out-of-time-ordered correlators (OTOCs) have emerged as a diagnostic of information scrambling and quantum chaos in many-body systems. We investigate the imprints of chaos in the dynamics of OTOCs in the Heisenberg spin-$1/2$ chain with random fields. The system is parameterized to exhibit a crossover from integrable to chaotic dynamics. We demonstrate numerically that the approach to saturation of the OTOC can distinguish between integrable and chaotic regimes, with a power-law $(1/t)$ relaxation for integrable systems and a higher-degree power-law decay $(1/t^α; α\ge 1)$ followed by an exponential relaxation for the chaotic regime. We further show that long-range spectral statistics, such as the number variance, are more effective in characterizing quantum chaos in the regime near saturation of OTOC. We also demonstrate that the relaxation and initial scrambling regimes exhibit distinct and universal features, with the former being sensitive and the latter being robust against different realizations of random-fields. The long-time saturation of OTOC also fluctuates with different realizations, and its exact expression is derived through the Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis.

### [52] [Ground state preparation of random all-to-all Hamiltonians using ADAPT-VQE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18339)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用TETRIS-ADAPT-VQE算法来构建随机哈密顿量的基态。

Result: 对于SYK模型（N=20），保真度≥99.3%；对于SK模型（L=18），保真度≥99.9998%。SK模型的基态制备在算子池大小和电路深度方面高效，而SYK模型（密集或中等稀疏）则效率不高。

Abstract: The ground state of random Hamiltonians with all-to-all interactions such as the quantum Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK) model and the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model follow volume-law entanglement and are expected to be hard to model using tensor networks. In recent years, some progress has been made to push the limit of classical methods using neural quantum states. However, it remains an open question whether there exist quantum algorithms that could offer a quantum advantage over the state-of-the-art classical methods in simulating random Hamiltonians. In this work, we show that one such algorithm, TETRIS-ADAPT-VQE, can construct accurate ground states for dense and sparse SYK models containing up to $N=20$ Majorana fermions achieving fidelities $\geq 99.3\%$ and for the quantum SK model with up to $L=18$ sites achieving fidelities $\geq 99.9998\%$. We find that while the preparation of ground states is efficient (in terms of operator pool size and circuit depth) for the SK model, it is not efficient for either dense or moderately sparse SYK models.

### [53] [Adiabatically-induced Kawaguchi geometry and jerk in quantum-classical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16037)
*Athanasios Chatzistavrakidis,Larisa Jonke,Ryan Requist*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过近恒等幺正变换序列 adiabatically 消除混合量子-经典系统中的量子自由度，推导出经典变量的有效作用量层级，发现三阶欧拉-拉格朗日方程是非牛顿的（力依赖于加加速度），并揭示了三阶项在经典变量空间上诱导出一种特殊的 Kawaguchi 几何（具有近辛结构和依赖于加速度的微分线元），可用于高效捕获分子动力学模拟中的高阶非绝热效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在混合量子-经典系统中，如何高效且准确地捕捉高阶非绝热效应是一个关键问题。传统的绝热近似仅考虑最低阶效应，而更高阶的修正对于精确分子动力学模拟至关重要。

Method: 对量子态施加一系列近恒等幺正变换，逐级消除量子自由度，从而推导出经典变量的有效作用量层级。该方法可对绝热参数进行任意阶展开。

Result: 三阶欧拉-拉格朗日方程是非牛顿的，力依赖于位置的三阶时间导数（加加速度）。三阶项在经典变量空间上诱导出一种特殊的 Kawaguchi 几何，其特征为近辛结构和依赖于加速度（而非仅速度）的微分线元。

Conclusion: 该层级化方法可应用于分子动力学模拟，以高效捕获高阶非绝热效应，为处理混合量子-经典系统中的非绝热动力学提供了新的几何框架和计算工具。

Abstract: Adiabatically eliminating the quantum degrees of freedom in a mixed quantum-classical system produces an effective force in the classical equation of motion. The elimination can be made to any order in the adiabatic parameter, generating a series of higher order forces. By applying a sequence of near-identity unitary transformations to the quantum state, we derive a hierarchy of increasingly accurate effective actions for the classical variables. The third order Euler-Lagrange equation is non-Newtonian as the force depends on the jerk, the third order time derivative of position. We find that the third order terms induce a special kind of Kawaguchi geometry on the space of classical variables. This geometry is characterized by an almost symplectic structure and a differential line element that depends on the acceleration in addition to the velocity. Our results can be used to efficiently capture higher order nonadiabatic effects in molecular dynamics simulations.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Quantum systems governed by unitary and reversible microscopic dynamics may nevertheless exhibit equilibration, in the sense that some effective description becomes time-independent. Standard equilibration results usually consider two separate situations: system-environment structures, in which the composite system evolves unitarily while the system of interest equilibrates, and restricted measurements, such as coarse-grained POVMs and observables, in which the measurement statistics equilibrate. Here, we bring these descriptions into a common state-level framework using the concept of generalized subsystems, where the accessible effective state appears as the output of a quantum channel acting on the microscopic state. We derive bounds showing that generalized subsystems equilibrate when their dimension is small compared with the effective dimension of the discarded microscopic information. We further show that this condition is met for typical initial states in large subspaces and that the resulting equilibrium description is largely insensitive to microscopic initial details. The framework recovers the usual equilibration bounds for ordinary subsystems and finite families of POVMs. As an example, we also introduce a finite-resolution energy channel that maps unresolved microscopic energy levels into effective energy levels, thereby making residual effective coherences explicit and showing how spectral multiplicities constrain those coherences while strengthening equilibration. Our results provide a unified state-level formulation of quantum equilibration under general forms of limited accessible information.

Abstract: We consider the problem of identifying a topological order based on bulk entanglement of the ground-state wavefunction. Previous work showed that some universal information can be extracted from multi-entropy measures, a class of multipartite entanglement measures obtained by applying permutation operators exchanging the degrees of freedom between different replicas of the wavefunction. It remains an open question to what extent such entanglement measures can be used to extract any universal information from the ground state. Here we show that the topological partition function $Z(M)$ of a manifold $M$ can be extracted provided that $M$ satisfies a topological condition which we term ``local achirality". Abstract: We characterize two nested Walsh parity-check filters implemented on Quandela's Belenos cloud photonic processor in a single-photon eight-mode spatial register. The modes are indexed by the vertices of the cube $Q_3$. These are first-quantized path/mode encodings of classical codes: the experiment verifies leakage suppression and syndrome routing, not error correction or protection against photon loss, and all probabilities are conditional on postselected single-photon detections. Across more than 340,000 detections, neutral inputs show residual DC-port leakage of $0.02\%$-$1.1\%$ (mean $0.6\%$), corresponding to $\approx21\times$ suppression relative to the ideal $0.125$ DC-capture baseline and $31.6\times$ relative to the measured non-neutral control. Injected DC contamination gives a monotonic soft error signal, and the three face-parity syndrome channels route to their predicted ports with $94$-$99\%$ selectivity. A sector-preserving unitary core keeps leakage far below non-neutral controls over one to three applications, with differences dominated by calibration and compilation systematics rather than gate-cycle physics. We quantify these limits, including fixed-pattern separator bias, $\pm 0.02$ calibration offsets, and compilation scatter near the $10^{-3}$ leakage level, and report a Hong-Ou-Mandel degradation episode in which suppression vanished and recovered after recalibration.

*Patrick Kelly,Victoria S. Ordonez,Michael R. Geller*

TL;DR: 本文提出通过Valiant-Vazirani定理的滤波预言机，将SAT问题归约为UNIQUE SAT，并利用扭矩非线性（如双分量BEC中的非线性）在多项式时间内求解NP问题（非#P），弥补了此前扭矩模型无法解决SAT的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展标准量子计算模型以包含非线性薛定谔方程的辅助自由度引起广泛关注，但实际实现的非线性（如扭矩模型）此前被认为无法解决SAT问题，本文旨在弥补这一差距。

Method: 构建Valiant-Vazirani定理的滤波预言机，提供从SAT到UNIQUE SAT的随机多项式时间归约；在无噪声极限下，利用扭矩非线性在多项式时间内求解UNIQUE SAT。

Result: 扭矩非线性可多项式时间求解NP问题，但无法求解#P问题；Quantum Valiant-Vazirani归约并不比经典版本更快。

Conclusion: 容错实现耦合模拟扭矩的非线性量子协处理器可实现NP问题的多项式时间求解，但#P问题仍不可解。

Abstract: There is growing interest in extensions of the standard model of gate-based quantum computation to include auxiliary degrees of freedom evolving according to a nonlinear Schrödinger equation. By reducing the Boolean satisfiability problem SAT to quantum state discrimination, Abrams and Lloyd argued that the right type of nonlinearity can be used to solve {\sf NP} and \#{\sf P} problems in polynomial time, at least in an idealized noise-free limit. For practical implementation, however, we are restricted to simulated and emergent nonlinearities, such as that appearing in mean field models for ultracold atoms and similar ensembles. A prominent example is the torsion model, which arises in two-component Bose-Einstein condensates and spin models with all-to-all Ising interaction. But torsion-based state discrimination appears to fall short of solving SAT. Here we close this gap by constructing the filtered oracle of the Valiant-Vazirani theorem, providing a randomized polynomial-time reduction from SAT to UNIQUE SAT, a promise problem where there is at most 1 satisfying assignment. In the noise free limit, the UNIQUE SAT problem can be olved in polynomial time using torsion nonlinearity. Quantum Valiant-Vazirani reduction is no faster than the efficient classical version, but a fault-tolerant implementation coupled to a nonlinear quantum coprocessor simulating torsion would enable polynomial time solution to {\sf NP} (but not \#{\sf P}) problems.

</details>


### [63] [Exact propagating Dirac wave packets in an attractive Coulomb-like potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18470)
*Siddhant Das*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次在外部势场（轴对称势 $V=-v_0/ρ$）中构造了狄拉克方程的精确、正能、可归一化波包解。其中一族仅由初等函数构成，其纵向轮廓在非相对论极限下重现自由薛定谔 Hermite-Gauss 波包。所有波包有两个显著特征：概率密度与自旋取向逐点解耦（尽管存在自旋-轨道耦合），以及在临界耦合 $v_0\to\hbar c/2$ 处时间演化完全冻结。此外还提出了将二维亥姆霍兹方程解映射为狄拉克波包的简单方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克方程在外部势场中精确的可归一化波包解此前尚未被构造出来，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在轴对称势 $V=-v_0/ρ$ 下求解狄拉克方程，构造正能、可归一化的波包解；并建立从二维亥姆霍兹方程到狄拉克波包的映射方案。

Result: 得到了首批精确狄拉克波包解，其中一族仅含初等函数，非相对论极限下退化为自由薛定谔 Hermite-Gauss 波包。发现概率密度与自旋解耦，且在 $v_0\to\hbar c/2$ 时波包时间演化完全冻结。

Conclusion: 成功构造了狄拉克方程在外部势场中的首批精确波包解，揭示了自旋解耦与临界冻结等新奇特性，并提供了进一步构造更多波包的系统性方法。

Abstract: We construct exact, positive-energy, normalizable wave-packet solutions of the Dirac equation in the axisymmetric potential $V=-\,v_0/ρ$ -- to our knowledge, the first such solutions in any external potential. Remarkably, one family comprises only elementary functions whose longitudinal profiles reproduce the free-Schrödinger Hermite--Gauss wave packets in the nonrelativistic limit. All packets share two striking features: (i) a probability density that is pointwise decoupled from spin orientation -- despite the inherent spin-orbit coupling of the Dirac equation -- and (ii) a complete freezing of their time evolution at the critical coupling $v_0\to\hbar c/2$. We also present a simple scheme that maps solutions of the 2D Helmholtz equation to further exact Dirac wave packets.

Abstract: In a standard two-level Ramsey interferometer, the measured phase accumulates linearly during the interrogation time. Here, we introduce three-level Ramsey interferometry that employs a noncyclic geometric phase response to enhance phase sensing, with projected internal-path interference reshaping the mapping from accumulated signal phase to readout phase. Near a geodesic-closure transition, a small accumulated signal phase produces a sharply amplified readout-phase shift. We quantify the accompanying gain--visibility tradeoff and identify a finite operating window in which the amplified response yields a net signal-to-noise-ratio gain under technical-noise-limited conditions. By tuning an initial Ramsey phase offset, this high-slope window can be positioned at a desired operating point and sampled repeatedly with shorter cycles, providing a geometric shortcut to improved projected stability. More broadly, these results establish a multilevel Ramsey route to enhanced phase sensitivity in quantum platforms, where two signal-collecting internal paths interfere to produce a noncyclic geometric response.

### [66] [Exponentially many initializations to avoid barren plateaus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18515)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有观点认为贫瘠高原是平均情况现象，可通过更仔细的初始化来避免。作者指出实际情况更为微妙，需要系统性地理解初始化策略与贫瘠高原之间的关系。

Method: 提出一阶矩框架，作为算子级别的诊断工具，用于判断初始化是否可能逃离完全集中的贫瘠高原不动点，并比较不同初始化策略导致的偏差。

Result: 该方法不仅复现了恒等初始化、高斯初始化等已知方案，还发现避免贫瘠高原并非唯一，存在大量偏移、有偏、非对称的参数分布可避免浓度问题，且这些选择不等价。可生成指数级多的不等价初始化策略家族。数值实验表明，不同一阶矩的初始化会导致不同的达到最小值。
